Senate Joint Resolution 2005 - Introduced


                                 SENATE JOINT RESOLUTION 

                                 SENATE JOINT RESOLUTION 
                                 SENATE JOINT RESOLUTION                                  SENATE JOINT RESOLUTION                                  BY  DAWSON

 SENATE JOINT RESOLUTION

  1 A Joint Resolution proposing amendments to the Constitution
  2    of the State of Iowa limiting years of service for members
  3    of the general assembly, the governor, and judges of the
  4    supreme court and court of appeals.
  5 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:
    TLSB 5959XS (4) 87
    ss/rj

PAG LIN



  1  1    Section 1.  The following amendment to the Constitution of
  1  2 the State of Iowa is proposed:
  1  3    1.  Section 3 of Article III of the Constitution of the State
  1  4 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1  5 Representatives == term limitation.SEC. 3.  The members of
  1  6 the house of representatives shall be chosen every second year,
  1  7 by the qualified electors of their respective districts, and
  1  8 their term of office shall commence on the first day of January
  1  9 next after their election, and continue two years, and until
  1 10 their successors are elected and qualified. A person shall
  1 11 not be elected for a term as representative if the term would
  1 12 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 13 in the general assembly. This limitation on years of service
  1 14 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 15 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 16 1, 2023.
  1 17    2.  Section 5 of Article III of the Constitution of the State
  1 18 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 19 Senators ==== qualifications == term limitation.SEC. 5.
  1 20    Senators shall be chosen for the term of four years, at
  1 21 the same time and place as representatives; they shall be
  1 22 twenty=five years of age, and possess the qualifications of
  1 23 representatives as to residence and citizenship. A person
  1 24 shall not be elected for a term as senator if the term would
  1 25 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 26 in the general assembly. This limitation on terms of service
  1 27 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 28 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 29 1, 2023.
  1 30    Sec. 2.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  1 31 State of Iowa is proposed:
  1 32    Section 6 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State of
  1 33 Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 34 Eligibility == term limitation.SEC. 6.  No person shall be
  1 35 eligible to the office of governor, or lieutenant governor,
  2  1 who shall not have been a citizen of the United States, and a
  2  2 resident of the state, two years next preceding the election,
  2  3 and attained the age of thirty years at the time of said
  2  4 election.
  2  5    A person shall not be elected for a term as governor if
  2  6 the term would result in the person serving more than a total
  2  7 of two terms as governor.  If a person is elevated to serve
  2  8 a portion of a term to which some other person was elected
  2  9 but that person died in office or resigned from office or was
  2 10 otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term served
  2 11 shall not be included in the terms of service for purposes
  2 12 of this limitation if the person did not serve for at least
  2 13 one=half of the four=year term.  This limitation on terms
  2 14 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  2 15 January 1, 2023.
  2 16    Sec. 3.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 17 State of Iowa is proposed:
  2 18    Section 17 of Article V of the Constitution of the State of
  2 19 Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  2 20 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2 21 Terms == judicial elections == term limitations.SEC. 17.
  2 22    Members of all courts shall have such tenure in office as may
  2 23 be fixed by law, but terms of supreme court judges shall be not
  2 24 less than eight years and terms of district court judges shall
  2 25 be not less than six years.  Judges shall serve for one year
  2 26 after appointment and until the first day of January following
  2 27 the next judicial election after the expiration of such year.
  2 28 They shall at such judicial election stand for retention in
  2 29 office on a separate ballot which shall submit the question of
  2 30 whether such judge shall be retained in office for the tenure
  2 31 prescribed for such office and when such tenure is a term of
  2 32 years, on their request, they shall, at the judicial election
  2 33 next before the end of each term, stand again for retention on
  2 34 such ballot.  Present supreme court and district court judges,
  2 35 at the expiration of their respective terms, may be retained
  3  1 in office in like manner for the tenure prescribed for such
  3  2 office.
  3  3    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed for
  3  4 a term as a supreme court judge if the term would result in the
  3  5 person serving more than a total of two full terms as a supreme
  3  6 court judge. This limitation on terms of service applies to
  3  7 terms of office beginning on or after January 1, 2023.
  3  8    The general assembly shall prescribe the time for holding
  3  9 judicial elections.
  3 10    Sec. 4.  The following amendments to the Constitution of the
  3 11 State of Iowa are proposed:
  3 12    1.  Section 1 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 13 of Iowa is amended to read as follows:
  3 14 Courts.SECTION 1.  The judicial power shall be vested in
  3 15 a supreme court,

  1 22 twenty=five years of age, and possess the qualifications of
  1 23 representatives as to residence and citizenship. A person
  1 24 shall not be elected for a term as senator if the term would
  1 25 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 26 in the general assembly. This limitation on terms of service
  1 27 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 28 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 29 1, 2023.
  1 30    Sec. 2.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  1 31 State of Iowa is proposed:
  1 32    Section 6 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State of
  1 33 Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 34 Eligibility == term limitation.SEC. 6.  No person shall be
  1 35 eligible to the office of governor, or lieutenant governor,
  2  1 who shall not have been a citizen of the United States, and a
  2  2 resident of the state, two years next preceding the election,
  2  3 and attained the age of thirty years at the time of said
  2  4 election.
  2  5    A person shall not be elected for a term as governor if
  2  6 the term would result in the person serving more than a total
  2  7 of two terms as governor.  If a person is elevated to serve
  2  8 a portion of a term to which some other person was elected
  2  9 but that person died in office or resigned from office or was
  2 10 otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term served
  2 11 shall not be included in the terms of service for purposes
  2 12 of this limitation if the person did not serve for at least
  2 13 one=half of the four=year term.  This limitation on terms
  2 14 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  2 15 January 1, 2023.
  2 16    Sec. 3.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 17 State of Iowa is proposed:
  2 18    Section 17 of Article V of the Constitution of the State of
  2 19 Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  2 20 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2 21 Terms == judicial elections == term limitations.SEC. 17.
  2 22    Members of all courts shall have such tenure in office as may
  2 23 be fixed by law, but terms of supreme court judges shall be not
  2 24 less than eight years and terms of district court judges shall
  2 25 be not less than six years.  Judges shall serve for one year
  2 26 after appointment and until the first day of January following
  2 27 the next judicial election after the expiration of such year.
  2 28 They shall at such judicial election stand for retention in
  2 29 office on a separate ballot which shall submit the question of
  2 30 whether such judge shall be retained in office for the tenure
  2 31 prescribed for such office and when such tenure is a term of
  2 32 years, on their request, they shall, at the judicial election
  2 33 next before the end of each term, stand again for retention on
  2 34 such ballot.  Present supreme court and district court judges,
  2 35 at the expiration of their respective terms, may be retained
  3  1 in office in like manner for the tenure prescribed for such
  3  2 office.
  3  3    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed for
  3  4 a term as a supreme court judge if the term would result in the
  3  5 person serving more than a total of two full terms as a supreme
  3  6 court judge. This limitation on terms of service applies to
  3  7 terms of office beginning on or after January 1, 2023.
  3  8    The general assembly shall prescribe the time for holding
  3  9 judicial elections.
  3 10    Sec. 4.  The following amendments to the Constitution of the
  3 11 State of Iowa are proposed:
  3 12    1.  Section 1 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 13 of Iowa is amended to read as follows:
  3 14 Courts.SECTION 1.  The judicial power shall be vested in
  3 15 a supreme court,   3    of the general assembly, the governor, and judges of the
  4    supreme court and court of appeals.
  5 BE IT RESOLVED BY THE GENERAL ASSEMBLY OF THE STATE OF IOWA:
    TLSB 5959XS (4) 87

  1  5 Representatives == term limitation.SEC. 3.  The members of
  1  6 the house of representatives shall be chosen every second year,
  1  7 by the qualified electors of their respective districts, and
  1  8 their term of office shall commence on the first day of January
  1  9 next after their election, and continue two years, and until
  1 10 their successors are elected and qualified. A person shall
  1 11 not be elected for a term as representative if the term would
  1 12 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 13 in the general assembly. This limitation on years of service
  1 14 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 15 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 16 1, 2023.

  1 18 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 19 Senators ==== qualifications == term limitation.SEC. 5.
  1 20    Senators shall be chosen for the term of four years, at
  1 21 the same time and place as representatives; they shall be
  1 22 twenty=five years of age, and possess the qualifications of
  1 23 representatives as to residence and citizenship. A person
  1 24 shall not be elected for a term as senator if the term would
  1 25 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 26 in the general assembly. This limitation on terms of service

  3  6 court judge. This limitation on terms of service applies to
  3  7 terms of office beginning on or after January 1, 2023.
  3  8    The general assembly shall prescribe the time for holding
  3  9 judicial elections.
  3 10    Sec. 4.  The following amendments to the Constitution of the
  3 11 State of Iowa are proposed:
  3 12    1.  Section 1 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 13 of Iowa is amended to read as follows:
  3 14 Courts.SECTION 1.  The judicial power shall be vested in
  3 15 a supreme court, 

  1  1    Section 1.  The following amendment to the Constitution of
  1  2 the State of Iowa is proposed:
  1  3    1.  Section 3 of Article III of the Constitution of the State
  1  4 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1  5 Representatives == term limitation.SEC. 3.  The members of
  1  6 the house of representatives shall be chosen every second year,
  1  7 by the qualified electors of their respective districts, and
  1  8 their term of office shall commence on the first day of January
  1  9 next after their election, and continue two years, and until
  1 10 their successors are elected and qualified. A person shall
  1 11 not be elected for a term as representative if the term would
  1 12 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 13 in the general assembly. This limitation on years of service
  1 14 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 15 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 16 1, 2023.
  1 17    2.  Section 5 of Article III of the Constitution of the State
  1 18 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 19 Senators ==== qualifications == term limitation.SEC. 5.
  1 20    Senators shall be chosen for the term of four years, at
  1 21 the same time and place as representatives; they shall be
  1 22 twenty=five years of age, and possess the qualifications of
  1 23 representatives as to residence and citizenship. A person
  1 24 shall not be elected for a term as senator if the term would
  1 25 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 26 in the general assembly. This limitation on terms of service
  1 27 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 28 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 29 1, 2023.
  1 30    Sec. 2.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  1 31 State of Iowa is proposed:
  1 32    Section 6 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State of
  1 33 Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 34 Eligibility == term limitation.SEC. 6.  No person shall be
  1 35 eligible to the office of governor, or lieutenant governor,
  2  1 who shall not have been a citizen of the United States, and a
  2  2 resident of the state, two years next preceding the election,
  2  3 and attained the age of thirty years at the time of said
  2  4 election.
  2  5    A person shall not be elected for a term as governor if
  2  6 the term would result in the person serving more than a total
  2  7 of two terms as governor.  If a person is elevated to serve
  2  8 a portion of a term to which some other person was elected
  2  9 but that person died in office or resigned from office or was
  2 10 otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term served
  2 11 shall not be included in the terms of service for purposes
  2 12 of this limitation if the person did not serve for at least
  2 13 one=half of the four=year term.  This limitation on terms
  2 14 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  2 15 January 1, 2023.
  2 16    Sec. 3.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 17 State of Iowa is proposed:
  2 18    Section 17 of Article V of the Constitution of the State of
  2 19 Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  2 20 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2 21 Terms == judicial elections == term limitations.SEC. 17.
  2 22    Members of all courts shall have such tenure in office as may
  2 23 be fixed by law, but terms of supreme court judges shall be not
  2 24 less than eight years and terms of district court judges shall
  2 25 be not less than six years.  Judges shall serve for one year
  2 26 after appointment and until the first day of January following
  2 27 the next judicial election after the expiration of such year.
  2 28 They shall at such judicial election stand for retention in
  2 29 office on a separate ballot which shall submit the question of
  2 30 whether such judge shall be retained in office for the tenure
  2 31 prescribed for such office and when such tenure is a term of
  2 32 years, on their request, they shall, at the judicial election
  2 33 next before the end of each term, stand again for retention on
  2 34 such ballot.  Present supreme court and district court judges,
  2 35 at the expiration of their respective terms, may be retained
  3  1 in office in like manner for the tenure prescribed for such
  3  2 office.
  3  3    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed for
  3  4 a term as a supreme court judge if the term would result in the
  3  5 person serving more than a total of two full terms as a supreme
  3  6 court judge. This limitation on terms of service applies to
  3  7 terms of office beginning on or after January 1, 2023.
  3  8    The general assembly shall prescribe the time for holding
  3  9 judicial elections.

  2 28 They shall at such judicial election stand for retention in
  2 29 office on a separate ballot which shall submit the question of
  2 30 whether such judge shall be retained in office for the tenure
  2 31 prescribed for such office and when such tenure is a term of
  2 32 years, on their request, they shall, at the judicial election
  2 33 next before the end of each term, stand again for retention on
  2 34 such ballot.  Present supreme court and district court judges,
  2 35 at the expiration of their respective terms, may be retained
  3  1 in office in like manner for the tenure prescribed for such
  3  2 office.
  3  3    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed for
  3  4 a term as a supreme court judge if the term would result in the
  3  5 person serving more than a total of two full terms as a supreme
  3  6 court judge. This limitation on terms of service applies to
  3  7 terms of office beginning on or after January 1, 2023.
  3  8    The general assembly shall prescribe the time for holding
  3  9 judicial elections.
  3 10    Sec. 4.  The following amendments to the Constitution of the
  3 11 State of Iowa are proposed:
  3 12    1.  Section 1 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 13 of Iowa is amended to read as follows:
  3 14 Courts.SECTION 1.  The judicial power shall be vested in
  3 15 a supreme court,   1  5 Representatives == term limitation.SEC. 3.  The members of
  1  6 the house of representatives shall be chosen every second year,
  1  7 by the qualified electors of their respective districts, and
  1  8 their term of office shall commence on the first day of January
  1  9 next after their election, and continue two years, and until
  1 10 their successors are elected and qualified. A person shall
  1 11 not be elected for a term as representative if the term would
  1 12 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 13 in the general assembly. This limitation on years of service
  1 14 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 15 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 16 1, 2023.
  1 17    2.  Section 5 of Article III of the Constitution of the State
  1 18 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 19 Senators ==== qualifications == term limitation.SEC. 5.
  1 20    Senators shall be chosen for the term of four years, at
  1 21 the same time and place as representatives; they shall be
  1 22 twenty=five years of age, and possess the qualifications of
  1 23 representatives as to residence and citizenship. A person
  1 24 shall not be elected for a term as senator if the term would
  1 25 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 26 in the general assembly. This limitation on terms of service
  1 27 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 28 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 29 1, 2023.
  1 30    Sec. 2.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  1 31 State of Iowa is proposed:
  1 32    Section 6 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State of
  1 33 Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 34 Eligibility == term limitation.SEC. 6.  No person shall be
  1 35 eligible to the office of governor, or lieutenant governor,
  2  1 who shall not have been a citizen of the United States, and a
  2  2 resident of the state, two years next preceding the election,
  2  3 and attained the age of thirty years at the time of said
  2  4 election.
  2  5    A person shall not be elected for a term as governor if
  2  6 the term would result in the person serving more than a total
  2  7 of two terms as governor.  If a person is elevated to serve
  2  8 a portion of a term to which some other person was elected
  2  9 but that person died in office or resigned from office or was
  2 10 otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term served
  2 11 shall not be included in the terms of service for purposes
  2 12 of this limitation if the person did not serve for at least
  2 13 one=half of the four=year term.  This limitation on terms
  2 14 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  2 15 January 1, 2023.

  2 20 following adopted in lieu thereof:

  2 23 be fixed by law, but terms of supreme court judges shall be not

  2 25 be not less than six years.  Judges shall serve for one year
  2 26 after appointment and until the first day of January following
  2 27 the next judicial election after the expiration of such year.

  2 29 office on a separate ballot which shall submit the question of
  2 30 whether such judge shall be retained in office for the tenure

  1 12 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 13 in the general assembly. This limitation on years of service
  1 14 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 15 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 16 1, 2023.
  1 17    2.  Section 5 of Article III of the Constitution of the State
  1 18 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 19 Senators ==== qualifications == term limitation.SEC. 5.
  1 20    Senators shall be chosen for the term of four years, at
  1 21 the same time and place as representatives; they shall be
  1 22 twenty=five years of age, and possess the qualifications of
  1 23 representatives as to residence and citizenship. A person
  1 24 shall not be elected for a term as senator if the term would
  1 25 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 26 in the general assembly. This limitation on terms of service
  1 27 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 28 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 29 1, 2023.
  1 30    Sec. 2.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  1 31 State of Iowa is proposed:
  1 32    Section 6 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State of
  1 33 Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 34 Eligibility == term limitation.SEC. 6.  No person shall be
  1 35 eligible to the office of governor, or lieutenant governor,
  2  1 who shall not have been a citizen of the United States, and a
  2  2 resident of the state, two years next preceding the election,
  2  3 and attained the age of thirty years at the time of said
  2  4 election.
  2  5    A person shall not be elected for a term as governor if
  2  6 the term would result in the person serving more than a total
  2  7 of two terms as governor.  If a person is elevated to serve
  2  8 a portion of a term to which some other person was elected
  2  9 but that person died in office or resigned from office or was
  2 10 otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term served
  2 11 shall not be included in the terms of service for purposes
  2 12 of this limitation if the person did not serve for at least
  2 13 one=half of the four=year term.  This limitation on terms
  2 14 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  2 15 January 1, 2023.
  2 16    Sec. 3.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 17 State of Iowa is proposed:
  2 18    Section 17 of Article V of the Constitution of the State of
  2 19 Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  2 20 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2 21 Terms == judicial elections == term limitations.SEC. 17.
  2 22    Members of all courts shall have such tenure in office as may
  2 23 be fixed by law, but terms of supreme court judges shall be not
  2 24 less than eight years and terms of district court judges shall
  2 25 be not less than six years.  Judges shall serve for one year
  2 26 after appointment and until the first day of January following
  2 27 the next judicial election after the expiration of such year.
  2 28 They shall at such judicial election stand for retention in
  2 29 office on a separate ballot which shall submit the question of
  2 30 whether such judge shall be retained in office for the tenure
  2 31 prescribed for such office and when such tenure is a term of
  2 32 years, on their request, they shall, at the judicial election
  2 33 next before the end of each term, stand again for retention on
  2 34 such ballot.  Present supreme court and district court judges,
  2 35 at the expiration of their respective terms, may be retained
  3  1 in office in like manner for the tenure prescribed for such
  3  2 office.
  3  3    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed for
  3  4 a term as a supreme court judge if the term would result in the
  3  5 person serving more than a total of two full terms as a supreme
  3  6 court judge. This limitation on terms of service applies to
  3  7 terms of office beginning on or after January 1, 2023.
  3  8    The general assembly shall prescribe the time for holding
  3  9 judicial elections.

  3  7 terms of office beginning on or after January 1, 2023.
  3  8    The general assembly shall prescribe the time for holding
  3  9 judicial elections.
  3 10    Sec. 4.  The following amendments to the Constitution of the
  3 11 State of Iowa are proposed:
  3 12    1.  Section 1 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 13 of Iowa is amended to read as follows:
  3 14 Courts.SECTION 1.  The judicial power shall be vested in
  3 15 a supreme court,   1 18 of Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 19 Senators ==== qualifications == term limitation.SEC. 5.
  1 20    Senators shall be chosen for the term of four years, at
  1 21 the same time and place as representatives; they shall be
  1 22 twenty=five years of age, and possess the qualifications of
  1 23 representatives as to residence and citizenship. A person
  1 24 shall not be elected for a term as senator if the term would
  1 25 result in the person serving more than a total of sixteen years
  1 26 in the general assembly. This limitation on terms of service
  1 27 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 28 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 29 1, 2023.
  1 30    Sec. 2.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  1 31 State of Iowa is proposed:
  1 32    Section 6 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State of
  1 33 Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 34 Eligibility == term limitation.SEC. 6.  No person shall be
  1 35 eligible to the office of governor, or lieutenant governor,
  2  1 who shall not have been a citizen of the United States, and a
  2  2 resident of the state, two years next preceding the election,
  2  3 and attained the age of thirty years at the time of said
  2  4 election.
  2  5    A person shall not be elected for a term as governor if
  2  6 the term would result in the person serving more than a total
  2  7 of two terms as governor.  If a person is elevated to serve
  2  8 a portion of a term to which some other person was elected
  2  9 but that person died in office or resigned from office or was
  2 10 otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term served
  2 11 shall not be included in the terms of service for purposes
  2 12 of this limitation if the person did not serve for at least
  2 13 one=half of the four=year term.  This limitation on terms
  2 14 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  2 15 January 1, 2023.
  2 16    Sec. 3.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 17 State of Iowa is proposed:
  2 18    Section 17 of Article V of the Constitution of the State of
  2 19 Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  2 20 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2 21 Terms == judicial elections == term limitations.SEC. 17.
  2 22    Members of all courts shall have such tenure in office as may
  2 23 be fixed by law, but terms of supreme court judges shall be not
  2 24 less than eight years and terms of district court judges shall
  2 25 be not less than six years.  Judges shall serve for one year
  2 26 after appointment and until the first day of January following
  2 27 the next judicial election after the expiration of such year.
  2 28 They shall at such judicial election stand for retention in
  2 29 office on a separate ballot which shall submit the question of
  2 30 whether such judge shall be retained in office for the tenure
  2 31 prescribed for such office and when such tenure is a term of
  2 32 years, on their request, they shall, at the judicial election
  2 33 next before the end of each term, stand again for retention on
  2 34 such ballot.  Present supreme court and district court judges,
  2 35 at the expiration of their respective terms, may be retained
  3  1 in office in like manner for the tenure prescribed for such
  3  2 office.
  3  3    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed for
  3  4 a term as a supreme court judge if the term would result in the
  3  5 person serving more than a total of two full terms as a supreme
  3  6 court judge. This limitation on terms of service applies to
  3  7 terms of office beginning on or after January 1, 2023.
  3  8    The general assembly shall prescribe the time for holding
  3  9 judicial elections.

  2 23 be fixed by law, but terms of supreme court judges shall be not
  2 24 less than eight years and terms of district court judges shall
  2 25 be not less than six years.  Judges shall serve for one year
  2 26 after appointment and until the first day of January following
  2 27 the next judicial election after the expiration of such year.
  2 28 They shall at such judicial election stand for retention in
  2 29 office on a separate ballot which shall submit the question of
  2 30 whether such judge shall be retained in office for the tenure
  2 31 prescribed for such office and when such tenure is a term of
  2 32 years, on their request, they shall, at the judicial election
  2 33 next before the end of each term, stand again for retention on
  2 34 such ballot.  Present supreme court and district court judges,
  2 35 at the expiration of their respective terms, may be retained
  3  1 in office in like manner for the tenure prescribed for such
  3  2 office.
  3  3    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed for
  3  4 a term as a supreme court judge if the term would result in the
  3  5 person serving more than a total of two full terms as a supreme
  3  6 court judge. This limitation on terms of service applies to
  3  7 terms of office beginning on or after January 1, 2023.
  3  8    The general assembly shall prescribe the time for holding
  3  9 judicial elections.
  3 10    Sec. 4.  The following amendments to the Constitution of the
  3 11 State of Iowa are proposed:
  3 12    1.  Section 1 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 13 of Iowa is amended to read as follows:
  3 14 Courts.SECTION 1.  The judicial power shall be vested in
  3 15 a supreme court,   1 26 in the general assembly. This limitation on terms of service
  1 27 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  1 28 2023, and for years of service occurring on or after January
  1 29 1, 2023.
  1 30    Sec. 2.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  1 31 State of Iowa is proposed:
  1 32    Section 6 of Article IV of the Constitution of the State of
  1 33 Iowa is repealed and the following adopted in lieu thereof:
  1 34 Eligibility == term limitation.SEC. 6.  No person shall be
  1 35 eligible to the office of governor, or lieutenant governor,
  2  1 who shall not have been a citizen of the United States, and a
  2  2 resident of the state, two years next preceding the election,
  2  3 and attained the age of thirty years at the time of said
  2  4 election.
  2  5    A person shall not be elected for a term as governor if
  2  6 the term would result in the person serving more than a total
  2  7 of two terms as governor.  If a person is elevated to serve
  2  8 a portion of a term to which some other person was elected
  2  9 but that person died in office or resigned from office or was
  2 10 otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term served
  2 11 shall not be included in the terms of service for purposes
  2 12 of this limitation if the person did not serve for at least
  2 13 one=half of the four=year term.  This limitation on terms
  2 14 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  2 15 January 1, 2023.

  2 15 January 1, 2023.
  2 16    Sec. 3.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 17 State of Iowa is proposed:
  2 18    Section 17 of Article V of the Constitution of the State of
  2 19 Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  2 20 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2 21 Terms == judicial elections == term limitations.SEC. 17.
  2 22    Members of all courts shall have such tenure in office as may
  2 23 be fixed by law, but terms of supreme court judges shall be not
  2 24 less than eight years and terms of district court judges shall
  2 25 be not less than six years.  Judges shall serve for one year
  2 26 after appointment and until the first day of January following
  2 27 the next judicial election after the expiration of such year.
  2 28 They shall at such judicial election stand for retention in
  2 29 office on a separate ballot which shall submit the question of
  2 30 whether such judge shall be retained in office for the tenure
  2 31 prescribed for such office and when such tenure is a term of
  2 32 years, on their request, they shall, at the judicial election
  2 33 next before the end of each term, stand again for retention on
  2 34 such ballot.  Present supreme court and district court judges,
  2 35 at the expiration of their respective terms, may be retained
  3  1 in office in like manner for the tenure prescribed for such
  3  2 office.
  3  3    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed for
  3  4 a term as a supreme court judge if the term would result in the
  3  5 person serving more than a total of two full terms as a supreme
  3  6 court judge. This limitation on terms of service applies to
  3  7 terms of office beginning on or after January 1, 2023.
  3  8    The general assembly shall prescribe the time for holding
  3  9 judicial elections.
  3 10    Sec. 4.  The following amendments to the Constitution of the
  3 11 State of Iowa are proposed:
  3 12    1.  Section 1 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  3 13 of Iowa is amended to read as follows:
  3 14 Courts.SECTION 1.  The judicial power shall be vested in
  3 15 a supreme court,   1 35 eligible to the office of governor, or lieutenant governor,
  2  1 who shall not have been a citizen of the United States, and a
  2  2 resident of the state, two years next preceding the election,
  2  3 and attained the age of thirty years at the time of said
  2  4 election.
  2  5    A person shall not be elected for a term as governor if
  2  6 the term would result in the person serving more than a total
  2  7 of two terms as governor.  If a person is elevated to serve
  2  8 a portion of a term to which some other person was elected
  2  9 but that person died in office or resigned from office or was
  2 10 otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term served
  2 11 shall not be included in the terms of service for purposes
  2 12 of this limitation if the person did not serve for at least
  2 13 one=half of the four=year term.  This limitation on terms
  2 14 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  2 15 January 1, 2023.

  3 14 Courts.SECTION 1.  The judicial power shall be vested in
  3 15 a supreme court,   2 10 otherwise removed from office, that portion of a term served
  2 11 shall not be included in the terms of service for purposes
  2 12 of this limitation if the person did not serve for at least
  2 13 one=half of the four=year term.  This limitation on terms
  2 14 of service applies to terms of office beginning on or after
  2 15 January 1, 2023.
  2 16    Sec. 3.  The following amendment to the Constitution of the
  2 17 State of Iowa is proposed:
  2 18    Section 17 of Article V of the Constitution of the State of
  2 19 Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  2 20 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  2 21 Terms == judicial elections == term limitations.SEC. 17.
  2 22    Members of all courts shall have such tenure in office as may
  2 23 be fixed by law, but terms of supreme court judges shall be not
  2 24 less than eight years and terms of district court judges shall
  2 25 be not less than six years.  Judges shall serve for one year
  2 26 after appointment and until the first day of January following
  2 27 the next judicial election after the expiration of such year.
  2 28 They shall at such judicial election stand for retention in
  2 29 office on a separate ballot which shall submit the question of
  2 30 whether such judge shall be retained in office for the tenure
  2 31 prescribed for such office and when such tenure is a term of
  2 32 years, on their request, they shall, at the judicial election
  2 33 next before the end of each term, stand again for retention on
  2 34 such ballot.  Present supreme court and district court judges,
  2 35 at the expiration of their respective terms, may be retained
  3  1 in office in like manner for the tenure prescribed for such
  3  2 office.
  3  3    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed for
  3  4 a term as a supreme court judge if the term would result in the
  3  5 person serving more than a total of two full terms as a supreme
  3  6 court judge. This limitation on terms of service applies to
  3  7 terms of office beginning on or after January 1, 2023.
  3  8    The general assembly shall prescribe the time for holding
  3  9 judicial elections.

  3 14 Courts.SECTION 1.  The judicial power shall be vested in

  2 29 office on a separate ballot which shall submit the question of

  4  2 supreme court   4  1 commission shall make nominations to fill vacancies in the
  4  2 supreme court   4  2 supreme court   4  3 and thereafter unless otherwise provided by law, the state
  4  4 judicial nominating commission shall be composed and selected
  4  5 as follows:  There shall be not less than three nor more than
  4  6 eight appointive members, as provided by law, and an equal
  4  7 number of elective members on such commission, all of whom
  4  8 shall be electors of the state.  The appointive members shall
  4  9 be appointed by the governor subject to confirmation by the
  4 10 senate.  The elective members shall be elected by the resident
  4 11 members of the bar of the state.  The judge of the supreme court
  4 12 who is senior in length of service on said court, other than
  4 13 the chief justice, shall also be a member of such commission
  4 14 and shall be its chairman.
  4 15    There shall be a district judicial nominating commission in
  4 16 each judicial district of the state.  Such commissions shall
  4 17 make nominations to fill vacancies in the district court within
  4 18 their respective districts.  Until July 4, 1973, and thereafter
  4 19 unless otherwise provided by law, district judicial nominating
  4 20 commissions shall be composed and selected as follows:  There
  4 21 shall be not less than three nor more than six appointive
  4 22 members, as provided by law, and an equal number of elective
  4 23 members on each such commission, all of whom shall be electors
  4 24 of the district.  The appointive members shall be appointed by
  4 25 the governor.  The elective members shall be elected by the
  4 26 resident members of the bar of the district.  The district
  4 27 judge of such district who is senior in length of service shall
  4 28 also be a member of such commission and shall be its chairman.
  4 29    Due consideration shall be given to area representation in
  4 30 the appointment and election of judicial nominating commission
  4 31 members.  Appointive and elective members of judicial
  4 32 nominating commissions shall serve for six=year terms, shall be
  4 33 ineligible for a second six=year term on the same commission,
  4 34 shall hold no office of profit of the United States or of the
  4 35 state during their terms, shall be chosen without reference to
  5  1 political affiliation, and shall have such other qualifications
  5  2 as may be prescribed by law.  As near as may be, the terms of
  5  3 one=third of such members shall expire every two years.
  5  4    4.  Section 18 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  5  5 of Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  5  6 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  5  7 Salaries == qualifications == retirement.SEC. 18.  Judges of
  5  8 the supreme court, court of appeals, and district court shall
  5  9 receive salaries from the state, shall be members of the bar
  5 10 of the state and shall have such other qualifications as may
  5 11 be prescribed by law.  Judges of the supreme court, court of
  5 12 appeals, and district court shall be ineligible to any other
  5 13 office of the state while serving on said court and for two
  5 14 years thereafter, except that appeals court judges and district
  5 15 court judges shall be eligible to the office of supreme court
  5 16 judge.  Other judicial officers shall be selected in such
  5 17 manner and shall have such tenure, compensation, and other
  5 18 qualification as may be fixed by law.  The general assembly
  5 19 shall prescribe mandatory retirement for judges of the supreme
  5 20 court, court of appeals, and district court at a specified
  5 21 age and shall provide for adequate retirement compensation.
  5 22 Retired judges may be subject to special assignment to
  5 23 temporary judicial duties by the supreme court, as provided by
  5 24 law.
  5 25    5.  Article V of the Constitution of the State of Iowa is
  5 26 amended by adding the following new section:
  5 27    SEC. 18A.  The court of appeals shall consist of such a
  5 28 number of judges and have such jurisdiction and tenure in
  5 29 office as may be fixed by law.
  5 30    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed
  5 31 for a term as a court of appeals judge if the term would result
  5 32 in the person serving more than a total of two full terms as a
  5 33 court of appeals judge. This limitation on terms of service
  5 34 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 35 2023.
  6  1    Sec. 5.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendments
  6  2 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa are referred to the
  6  3 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  6  4 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  6  5 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  6  6 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  6  7 provided by law.
  6  8                           EXPLANATION
  6  9 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  6 10 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  6 11    This joint resolution proposes four amendments to the
  6 12 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting years of service
  6 13 for persons elected to the general assembly, office of the
  6 14 governor, supreme court, or court of appeals, and establishing
  6 15 the court of appeals in the constitution.
  6 16    The first amendment provides that a person shall not be
  6 17 elected for a term as a representative or senator if the term
  6 18 would result in the person serving more than 16 years in the
  6 19 general assembly.
  6 20    The second proposed amendment provides that a person shall
  6 21 not be elected for a term as governor if the term would result
  6 22 in the person serving more than two terms as governor. For the
  6 23 purposes of this limitation, a person shall not be considered
  6 24 to have served a term if that person was elevated to serve a
  6 25 portion of a term as governor if that person did not serve at
  6 26 least one=half of the full term.
  6 27    The third proposed amendment provides that a person shall
  6 28 not be elected or appointed to serve as a judge on the supreme
  6 29 court if the term would result in the person serving more than
  6 30 two full terms as a judge on the supreme court.
  6 31    The fourth proposed amendment establishes the court of
  6 32 appeals in the Constitution of the State of Iowa, provides that
  6 33 three nominees for each vacancy in the court shall be submitted
  6 34 by the state judicial nominating commission, from which the
  6 35 governor shall select an appointee and provides for the payment
  7  1 of a salary to judges of the court, the establishment of a
  7  2 mandatory retirement age, and a limitation on holding any other
  7  3 office of the state until two years after retiring from the
  7  4 court. The amendment provides that the court of appeals shall
  7  5 consist of such a number of judges and have such jurisdiction
  7  6 and term in office as may be fixed by law. The amendment also
  7  7 provides that a person shall not be elected or appointed to
  7  8 serve as a judge on the court of appeals if the term would
  7  9 result in the person serving more than two terms as a judge on
  7 10 the court of appeals.
  7 11    The amendment applies to terms of office beginning on or
  7 12 after January 1, 2023, and for years of service occurring on or
  7 13 after January 1, 2023.
  7 14    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  7 15 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  7 16 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5959XS (4) 87
       ss/rj
  4  4 judicial nominating commission shall be composed and selected
  4  5 as follows:  There shall be not less than three nor more than
  4  6 eight appointive members, as provided by law, and an equal
  4  7 number of elective members on such commission, all of whom
  4  8 shall be electors of the state.  The appointive members shall
  4  9 be appointed by the governor subject to confirmation by the
  4 10 senate.  The elective members shall be elected by the resident
  4 11 members of the bar of the state.  The judge of the supreme court
  4 12 who is senior in length of service on said court, other than
  4 13 the chief justice, shall also be a member of such commission
  4 14 and shall be its chairman.
  4 15    There shall be a district judicial nominating commission in
  4 16 each judicial district of the state.  Such commissions shall
  4 17 make nominations to fill vacancies in the district court within
  4 18 their respective districts.  Until July 4, 1973, and thereafter
  4 19 unless otherwise provided by law, district judicial nominating
  4 20 commissions shall be composed and selected as follows:  There
  4 21 shall be not less than three nor more than six appointive
  4 22 members, as provided by law, and an equal number of elective
  4 23 members on each such commission, all of whom shall be electors
  4 24 of the district.  The appointive members shall be appointed by
  4 25 the governor.  The elective members shall be elected by the
  4 26 resident members of the bar of the district.  The district
  4 27 judge of such district who is senior in length of service shall
  4 28 also be a member of such commission and shall be its chairman.
  4 29    Due consideration shall be given to area representation in
  4 30 the appointment and election of judicial nominating commission
  4 31 members.  Appointive and elective members of judicial
  4 32 nominating commissions shall serve for six=year terms, shall be
  4 33 ineligible for a second six=year term on the same commission,
  4 34 shall hold no office of profit of the United States or of the
  4 35 state during their terms, shall be chosen without reference to
  5  1 political affiliation, and shall have such other qualifications
  5  2 as may be prescribed by law.  As near as may be, the terms of
  5  3 one=third of such members shall expire every two years.
  5  4    4.  Section 18 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  5  5 of Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  5  6 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  5  7 Salaries == qualifications == retirement.SEC. 18.  Judges of
  5  8 the supreme court, court of appeals, and district court shall
  5  9 receive salaries from the state, shall be members of the bar
  5 10 of the state and shall have such other qualifications as may
  5 11 be prescribed by law.  Judges of the supreme court, court of
  5 12 appeals, and district court shall be ineligible to any other
  5 13 office of the state while serving on said court and for two
  5 14 years thereafter, except that appeals court judges and district
  5 15 court judges shall be eligible to the office of supreme court
  5 16 judge.  Other judicial officers shall be selected in such
  5 17 manner and shall have such tenure, compensation, and other
  5 18 qualification as may be fixed by law.  The general assembly
  5 19 shall prescribe mandatory retirement for judges of the supreme
  5 20 court, court of appeals, and district court at a specified
  5 21 age and shall provide for adequate retirement compensation.
  5 22 Retired judges may be subject to special assignment to
  5 23 temporary judicial duties by the supreme court, as provided by
  5 24 law.
  5 25    5.  Article V of the Constitution of the State of Iowa is
  5 26 amended by adding the following new section:
  5 27    SEC. 18A.  The court of appeals shall consist of such a
  5 28 number of judges and have such jurisdiction and tenure in
  5 29 office as may be fixed by law.
  5 30    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed
  5 31 for a term as a court of appeals judge if the term would result
  5 32 in the person serving more than a total of two full terms as a
  5 33 court of appeals judge. This limitation on terms of service
  5 34 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 35 2023.
  6  1    Sec. 5.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendments
  6  2 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa are referred to the
  6  3 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  6  4 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  6  5 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  6  6 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  6  7 provided by law.
  6  8                           EXPLANATION

  6 35 governor shall select an appointee and provides for the payment
  7  1 of a salary to judges of the court, the establishment of a
  7  2 mandatory retirement age, and a limitation on holding any other
  7  3 office of the state until two years after retiring from the
  7  4 court. The amendment provides that the court of appeals shall
  7  5 consist of such a number of judges and have such jurisdiction
  7  6 and term in office as may be fixed by law. The amendment also
  7  7 provides that a person shall not be elected or appointed to
  7  8 serve as a judge on the court of appeals if the term would
  7  9 result in the person serving more than two terms as a judge on
  7 10 the court of appeals.
  7 11    The amendment applies to terms of office beginning on or
  7 12 after January 1, 2023, and for years of service occurring on or
  7 13 after January 1, 2023.
  7 14    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  7 15 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  7 16 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5959XS (4) 87
       ss/rj
  4  8 shall be electors of the state.  The appointive members shall
  4  9 be appointed by the governor subject to confirmation by the
  4 10 senate.  The elective members shall be elected by the resident
  4 11 members of the bar of the state.  The judge of the supreme court
  4 12 who is senior in length of service on said court, other than
  4 13 the chief justice, shall also be a member of such commission
  4 14 and shall be its chairman.
  4 15    There shall be a district judicial nominating commission in
  4 16 each judicial district of the state.  Such commissions shall
  4 17 make nominations to fill vacancies in the district court within
  4 18 their respective districts.  Until July 4, 1973, and thereafter
  4 19 unless otherwise provided by law, district judicial nominating
  4 20 commissions shall be composed and selected as follows:  There
  4 21 shall be not less than three nor more than six appointive
  4 22 members, as provided by law, and an equal number of elective
  4 23 members on each such commission, all of whom shall be electors
  4 24 of the district.  The appointive members shall be appointed by
  4 25 the governor.  The elective members shall be elected by the
  4 26 resident members of the bar of the district.  The district
  4 27 judge of such district who is senior in length of service shall
  4 28 also be a member of such commission and shall be its chairman.
  4 29    Due consideration shall be given to area representation in
  4 30 the appointment and election of judicial nominating commission
  4 31 members.  Appointive and elective members of judicial
  4 32 nominating commissions shall serve for six=year terms, shall be
  4 33 ineligible for a second six=year term on the same commission,
  4 34 shall hold no office of profit of the United States or of the
  4 35 state during their terms, shall be chosen without reference to
  5  1 political affiliation, and shall have such other qualifications
  5  2 as may be prescribed by law.  As near as may be, the terms of
  5  3 one=third of such members shall expire every two years.
  5  4    4.  Section 18 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  5  5 of Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  5  6 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  5  7 Salaries == qualifications == retirement.SEC. 18.  Judges of
  5  8 the supreme court, court of appeals, and district court shall
  5  9 receive salaries from the state, shall be members of the bar
  5 10 of the state and shall have such other qualifications as may
  5 11 be prescribed by law.  Judges of the supreme court, court of
  5 12 appeals, and district court shall be ineligible to any other
  5 13 office of the state while serving on said court and for two
  5 14 years thereafter, except that appeals court judges and district
  5 15 court judges shall be eligible to the office of supreme court
  5 16 judge.  Other judicial officers shall be selected in such
  5 17 manner and shall have such tenure, compensation, and other
  5 18 qualification as may be fixed by law.  The general assembly
  5 19 shall prescribe mandatory retirement for judges of the supreme
  5 20 court, court of appeals, and district court at a specified
  5 21 age and shall provide for adequate retirement compensation.
  5 22 Retired judges may be subject to special assignment to
  5 23 temporary judicial duties by the supreme court, as provided by
  5 24 law.
  5 25    5.  Article V of the Constitution of the State of Iowa is
  5 26 amended by adding the following new section:
  5 27    SEC. 18A.  The court of appeals shall consist of such a
  5 28 number of judges and have such jurisdiction and tenure in
  5 29 office as may be fixed by law.
  5 30    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed
  5 31 for a term as a court of appeals judge if the term would result
  5 32 in the person serving more than a total of two full terms as a
  5 33 court of appeals judge. This limitation on terms of service
  5 34 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 35 2023.
  6  1    Sec. 5.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendments
  6  2 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa are referred to the
  6  3 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  6  4 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  6  5 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  6  6 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  6  7 provided by law.
  6  8                           EXPLANATION
  6  9 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  6 10 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  6 11    This joint resolution proposes four amendments to the
  6 12 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting years of service
  6 13 for persons elected to the general assembly, office of the
  6 14 governor, supreme court, or court of appeals, and establishing
  6 15 the court of appeals in the constitution.
  6 16    The first amendment provides that a person shall not be
  6 17 elected for a term as a representative or senator if the term
  6 18 would result in the person serving more than 16 years in the
  6 19 general assembly.
  6 20    The second proposed amendment provides that a person shall
  6 21 not be elected for a term as governor if the term would result
  6 22 in the person serving more than two terms as governor. For the
  6 23 purposes of this limitation, a person shall not be considered
  6 24 to have served a term if that person was elevated to serve a
  6 25 portion of a term as governor if that person did not serve at
  6 26 least one=half of the full term.
  6 27    The third proposed amendment provides that a person shall
  6 28 not be elected or appointed to serve as a judge on the supreme
  6 29 court if the term would result in the person serving more than
  6 30 two full terms as a judge on the supreme court.
  6 31    The fourth proposed amendment establishes the court of
  6 32 appeals in the Constitution of the State of Iowa, provides that
  6 33 three nominees for each vacancy in the court shall be submitted
  6 34 by the state judicial nominating commission, from which the
  6 35 governor shall select an appointee and provides for the payment
  7  1 of a salary to judges of the court, the establishment of a
  7  2 mandatory retirement age, and a limitation on holding any other
  7  3 office of the state until two years after retiring from the
  7  4 court. The amendment provides that the court of appeals shall
  7  5 consist of such a number of judges and have such jurisdiction
  7  6 and term in office as may be fixed by law. The amendment also
  7  7 provides that a person shall not be elected or appointed to
  7  8 serve as a judge on the court of appeals if the term would
  7  9 result in the person serving more than two terms as a judge on
  7 10 the court of appeals.
  7 11    The amendment applies to terms of office beginning on or
  7 12 after January 1, 2023, and for years of service occurring on or
  7 13 after January 1, 2023.
  7 14    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  7 15 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  7 16 electorate for ratification.

  4 35 state during their terms, shall be chosen without reference to
  5  1 political affiliation, and shall have such other qualifications
  5  2 as may be prescribed by law.  As near as may be, the terms of
  5  3 one=third of such members shall expire every two years.
  5  4    4.  Section 18 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  5  5 of Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  5  6 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  5  7 Salaries == qualifications == retirement.SEC. 18.  Judges of
  5  8 the supreme court, court of appeals, and district court shall
  5  9 receive salaries from the state, shall be members of the bar
  5 10 of the state and shall have such other qualifications as may
  5 11 be prescribed by law.  Judges of the supreme court, court of
  5 12 appeals, and district court shall be ineligible to any other
  5 13 office of the state while serving on said court and for two
  5 14 years thereafter, except that appeals court judges and district
  5 15 court judges shall be eligible to the office of supreme court
  5 16 judge.  Other judicial officers shall be selected in such
  5 17 manner and shall have such tenure, compensation, and other
  5 18 qualification as may be fixed by law.  The general assembly
  5 19 shall prescribe mandatory retirement for judges of the supreme
  5 20 court, court of appeals, and district court at a specified
  5 21 age and shall provide for adequate retirement compensation.
  5 22 Retired judges may be subject to special assignment to
  5 23 temporary judicial duties by the supreme court, as provided by
  5 24 law.
  5 25    5.  Article V of the Constitution of the State of Iowa is
  5 26 amended by adding the following new section:
  5 27    SEC. 18A.  The court of appeals shall consist of such a
  5 28 number of judges and have such jurisdiction and tenure in
  5 29 office as may be fixed by law.
  5 30    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed
  5 31 for a term as a court of appeals judge if the term would result
  5 32 in the person serving more than a total of two full terms as a
  5 33 court of appeals judge. This limitation on terms of service
  5 34 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 35 2023.
  6  1    Sec. 5.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendments
  6  2 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa are referred to the
  6  3 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  6  4 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  6  5 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  6  6 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  6  7 provided by law.
  6  8                           EXPLANATION
  6  9 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  6 10 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  6 11    This joint resolution proposes four amendments to the
  6 12 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting years of service
  6 13 for persons elected to the general assembly, office of the
  6 14 governor, supreme court, or court of appeals, and establishing
  6 15 the court of appeals in the constitution.
  6 16    The first amendment provides that a person shall not be
  6 17 elected for a term as a representative or senator if the term
  6 18 would result in the person serving more than 16 years in the
  6 19 general assembly.
  6 20    The second proposed amendment provides that a person shall
  6 21 not be elected for a term as governor if the term would result
  6 22 in the person serving more than two terms as governor. For the
  6 23 purposes of this limitation, a person shall not be considered
  6 24 to have served a term if that person was elevated to serve a
  6 25 portion of a term as governor if that person did not serve at
  6 26 least one=half of the full term.
  6 27    The third proposed amendment provides that a person shall
  6 28 not be elected or appointed to serve as a judge on the supreme
  6 29 court if the term would result in the person serving more than
  6 30 two full terms as a judge on the supreme court.
  6 31    The fourth proposed amendment establishes the court of
  6 32 appeals in the Constitution of the State of Iowa, provides that
  6 33 three nominees for each vacancy in the court shall be submitted
  6 34 by the state judicial nominating commission, from which the
  6 35 governor shall select an appointee and provides for the payment
  7  1 of a salary to judges of the court, the establishment of a
  7  2 mandatory retirement age, and a limitation on holding any other
  7  3 office of the state until two years after retiring from the
  7  4 court. The amendment provides that the court of appeals shall
  7  5 consist of such a number of judges and have such jurisdiction
  7  6 and term in office as may be fixed by law. The amendment also
  7  7 provides that a person shall not be elected or appointed to
  7  8 serve as a judge on the court of appeals if the term would
  7  9 result in the person serving more than two terms as a judge on
  7 10 the court of appeals.
  7 11    The amendment applies to terms of office beginning on or
  7 12 after January 1, 2023, and for years of service occurring on or
  7 13 after January 1, 2023.
  7 14    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  7 15 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  7 16 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5959XS (4) 87
       ss/rj
  4 13 the chief justice, shall also be a member of such commission
  4 14 and shall be its chairman.
  4 15    There shall be a district judicial nominating commission in
  4 16 each judicial district of the state.  Such commissions shall
  4 17 make nominations to fill vacancies in the district court within
  4 18 their respective districts.  Until July 4, 1973, and thereafter
  4 19 unless otherwise provided by law, district judicial nominating
  4 20 commissions shall be composed and selected as follows:  There
  4 21 shall be not less than three nor more than six appointive
  4 22 members, as provided by law, and an equal number of elective
  4 23 members on each such commission, all of whom shall be electors
  4 24 of the district.  The appointive members shall be appointed by
  4 25 the governor.  The elective members shall be elected by the
  4 26 resident members of the bar of the district.  The district
  4 27 judge of such district who is senior in length of service shall
  4 28 also be a member of such commission and shall be its chairman.
  4 29    Due consideration shall be given to area representation in
  4 30 the appointment and election of judicial nominating commission
  4 31 members.  Appointive and elective members of judicial
  4 32 nominating commissions shall serve for six=year terms, shall be
  4 33 ineligible for a second six=year term on the same commission,
  4 34 shall hold no office of profit of the United States or of the
  4 35 state during their terms, shall be chosen without reference to
  5  1 political affiliation, and shall have such other qualifications
  5  2 as may be prescribed by law.  As near as may be, the terms of
  5  3 one=third of such members shall expire every two years.
  5  4    4.  Section 18 of Article V of the Constitution of the State

  5 23 temporary judicial duties by the supreme court, as provided by

  6 28 not be elected or appointed to serve as a judge on the supreme
  6 29 court if the term would result in the person serving more than
  6 30 two full terms as a judge on the supreme court.
  6 31    The fourth proposed amendment establishes the court of
  6 32 appeals in the Constitution of the State of Iowa, provides that
  6 33 three nominees for each vacancy in the court shall be submitted
  6 34 by the state judicial nominating commission, from which the
  6 35 governor shall select an appointee and provides for the payment
  7  1 of a salary to judges of the court, the establishment of a
  7  2 mandatory retirement age, and a limitation on holding any other
  7  3 office of the state until two years after retiring from the
  7  4 court. The amendment provides that the court of appeals shall
  7  5 consist of such a number of judges and have such jurisdiction
  7  6 and term in office as may be fixed by law. The amendment also
  7  7 provides that a person shall not be elected or appointed to
  7  8 serve as a judge on the court of appeals if the term would
  7  9 result in the person serving more than two terms as a judge on
  7 10 the court of appeals.
  7 11    The amendment applies to terms of office beginning on or
  7 12 after January 1, 2023, and for years of service occurring on or
  7 13 after January 1, 2023.
  7 14    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  7 15 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  7 16 electorate for ratification.
       LSB 5959XS (4) 87
       ss/rj
  4 17 make nominations to fill vacancies in the district court within
  4 18 their respective districts.  Until July 4, 1973, and thereafter
  4 19 unless otherwise provided by law, district judicial nominating
  4 20 commissions shall be composed and selected as follows:  There
  4 21 shall be not less than three nor more than six appointive
  4 22 members, as provided by law, and an equal number of elective
  4 23 members on each such commission, all of whom shall be electors
  4 24 of the district.  The appointive members shall be appointed by
  4 25 the governor.  The elective members shall be elected by the
  4 26 resident members of the bar of the district.  The district
  4 27 judge of such district who is senior in length of service shall
  4 28 also be a member of such commission and shall be its chairman.
  4 29    Due consideration shall be given to area representation in
  4 30 the appointment and election of judicial nominating commission
  4 31 members.  Appointive and elective members of judicial
  4 32 nominating commissions shall serve for six=year terms, shall be
  4 33 ineligible for a second six=year term on the same commission,
  4 34 shall hold no office of profit of the United States or of the
  4 35 state during their terms, shall be chosen without reference to
  5  1 political affiliation, and shall have such other qualifications
  5  2 as may be prescribed by law.  As near as may be, the terms of
  5  3 one=third of such members shall expire every two years.
  5  4    4.  Section 18 of Article V of the Constitution of the State
  5  5 of Iowa, as added by the Amendment of 1962, is repealed and the
  5  6 following adopted in lieu thereof:
  5  7 Salaries == qualifications == retirement.SEC. 18.  Judges of
  5  8 the supreme court, court of appeals, and district court shall
  5  9 receive salaries from the state, shall be members of the bar
  5 10 of the state and shall have such other qualifications as may
  5 11 be prescribed by law.  Judges of the supreme court, court of
  5 12 appeals, and district court shall be ineligible to any other
  5 13 office of the state while serving on said court and for two
  5 14 years thereafter, except that appeals court judges and district
  5 15 court judges shall be eligible to the office of supreme court
  5 16 judge.  Other judicial officers shall be selected in such
  5 17 manner and shall have such tenure, compensation, and other
  5 18 qualification as may be fixed by law.  The general assembly
  5 19 shall prescribe mandatory retirement for judges of the supreme
  5 20 court, court of appeals, and district court at a specified
  5 21 age and shall provide for adequate retirement compensation.
  5 22 Retired judges may be subject to special assignment to
  5 23 temporary judicial duties by the supreme court, as provided by
  5 24 law.
  5 25    5.  Article V of the Constitution of the State of Iowa is
  5 26 amended by adding the following new section:
  5 27    SEC. 18A.  The court of appeals shall consist of such a
  5 28 number of judges and have such jurisdiction and tenure in
  5 29 office as may be fixed by law.
  5 30    A person shall not be eligible to be elected or appointed
  5 31 for a term as a court of appeals judge if the term would result
  5 32 in the person serving more than a total of two full terms as a
  5 33 court of appeals judge. This limitation on terms of service
  5 34 applies to terms of office beginning on or after January 1,
  5 35 2023.
  6  1    Sec. 5.  REFERRAL AND PUBLICATION.  The foregoing amendments
  6  2 to the Constitution of the State of Iowa are referred to the
  6  3 general assembly to be chosen at the next general election
  6  4 for members of the general assembly, and the secretary of
  6  5 state is directed to cause the same to be published for three
  6  6 consecutive months previous to the date of that election as
  6  7 provided by law.
  6  8                           EXPLANATION
  6  9 The inclusion of this explanation does not constitute agreement with
  6 10 the explanation's substance by the members of the general assembly.
  6 11    This joint resolution proposes four amendments to the
  6 12 Constitution of the State of Iowa limiting years of service
  6 13 for persons elected to the general assembly, office of the
  6 14 governor, supreme court, or court of appeals, and establishing
  6 15 the court of appeals in the constitution.
  6 16    The first amendment provides that a person shall not be
  6 17 elected for a term as a representative or senator if the term
  6 18 would result in the person serving more than 16 years in the
  6 19 general assembly.
  6 20    The second proposed amendment provides that a person shall
  6 21 not be elected for a term as governor if the term would result
  6 22 in the person serving more than two terms as governor. For the
  6 23 purposes of this limitation, a person shall not be considered
  6 24 to have served a term if that person was elevated to serve a
  6 25 portion of a term as governor if that person did not serve at
  6 26 least one=half of the full term.
  6 27    The third proposed amendment provides that a person shall
  6 28 not be elected or appointed to serve as a judge on the supreme
  6 29 court if the term would result in the person serving more than
  6 30 two full terms as a judge on the supreme court.
  6 31    The fourth proposed amendment establishes the court of
  6 32 appeals in the Constitution of the State of Iowa, provides that
  6 33 three nominees for each vacancy in the court shall be submitted
  6 34 by the state judicial nominating commission, from which the
  6 35 governor shall select an appointee and provides for the payment
  7  1 of a salary to judges of the court, the establishment of a
  7  2 mandatory retirement age, and a limitation on holding any other
  7  3 office of the state until two years after retiring from the
  7  4 court. The amendment provides that the court of appeals shall
  7  5 consist of such a number of judges and have such jurisdiction
  7  6 and term in office as may be fixed by law. The amendment also
  7  7 provides that a person shall not be elected or appointed to
  7  8 serve as a judge on the court of appeals if the term would
  7  9 result in the person serving more than two terms as a judge on
  7 10 the court of appeals.
  7 11    The amendment applies to terms of office beginning on or
  7 12 after January 1, 2023, and for years of service occurring on or
  7 13 after January 1, 2023.
  7 14    The resolution, if adopted, would be referred to the next
  7 15 general assembly for adoption before being submitted to the
  7 16 electorate for ratification.
